THE DONKEY CABBAGE There be once a young Hunter who go boldly into the forest .
He have a merry and light heart , and a he go whistle along there come an ugly old woman , who say to him , ` Good-day , dear hunter !
You be very merry and contented , but I suffer hunger and thirst , so give me a trifle . '
The Hunter be sorry for the poor old woman , and he felt in his pocket and give her all he could spare .
He be go on then , but the old woman stop him and say , ` Listen , dear hunter , to what I say .
Because of your kind heart I will make you a present .
Go on your way , and in a short time you will come to a tree on which sit nine bird who have a cloak in their claw and be quarrel over it .
Then take aim with your gun and shoot in the middle of them ; they will let the cloak fall , but one of the bird will be hit and will drop down dead .
Take the cloak with you ; it be a wishing-cloak , and when you throw it on your shoulder you have only to wish yourself at a certain place , and in the twinkling of an eye you be there .
Take the heart out of the dead bird and swallow it whole , and early every morning when you get up you will find a gold piece under your pillow . '
The Hunter thank the wise woman , and think to himself ` These be splendid thing she have promise me , if only they come to pass ! '
So he walk on about a hundred yard , and then he hear above him in the branch such a screaming and chirping that he look up , and there he saw a heap of bird tear a cloth with their beak and foot , shriek , tug , and fight , a if each want it for himself .
` Well , ' say the Hunter , ` this be wonderful !
It be just a the old woman say ' ; and he take his gun on his shoulder , pull the trigger , and shot into the midst of them , so that their feather fly about .
Then the flock take flight with much screaming , but one fell dead , and the cloak flutter down .
Then the Hunter do a the old woman have tell him : he cut open the bird , find it heart , swallow it , and take the cloak home with him .
The next morning when he awake he remember the promise , and want to see if it have come true .
But when he lift up his pillow , there sparkle the gold piece , and the next morning he find another , and so on every time he get up .
He collect a heap of gold , but at last he think to himself , ` What good be all my gold to me if I stay at home ?
I will travel and look a bit about me in the world . '
So he take leave of his parent , sling his hunt knapsack and his gun round him , and journey into the world .
It happen that one day he go through a thick wood , and when he come to the end of it there lay in the plain before him a large castle .
At one of the window in it stand an old woman with a most beautiful maiden by her side , look out .
But the old woman be a witch , and she say to the girl , ` There come one out of the wood who have a wonderful treasure in his body which we must manage to possess ourselves of , darling daughter ; we have more right to it than he .
He have a bird 's heart in him , and so every morning there lie a gold piece under his pillow . '
She tell her how they could get hold of it , and how she be to coax it from him , and at last threaten her angrily , say , ` And if you do not obey me , you shall repent it ! '
When the Hunter come nearer he saw the maiden , and say to himself , ' I have travel so far now that I will rest , and turn into this beautiful castle ; money I have in plenty . '
But the real reason be that he have catch sight of the lovely face .
He go into the house , and be kindly receive and hospitably entertain .
It be not long before he be so much in love with the witch-maiden that he think of nothing else , and only look in her eye , and whatever she want , that he gladly do .
Then the old witch say , ` Now we must have the bird-heart ; he will not feel when it be go . '
She prepare a drink , and when it be ready she pour it in a goblet and give it to the maiden , who have to hand it to the hunter .
` Drink to me now , my dear , ' she say .
Then he take the goblet , and when he have swallow the drink the bird-heart come out of his mouth .
The maiden have to get hold of it secretly and then swallow it herself , for the old witch want to have it .
Thenceforward he find no more gold under his pillow , and it lay under the maiden 's ; but he be so much in love and so much bewitch that he think of nothing except spend all his time with the maiden .
Then the old witch say , ` We have the bird-heart , but we must also get the wishing-cloak from him . '
The maiden answer , ` We will leave him that ; he have already lose his wealth ! '
The old witch grow angry , and say , ` Such a cloak be a wonderful thing , it be seldom to be have in the world , and have it I must and will . '
She beat the maiden , and say that if she do not obey it would go ill with her .
So she do her mother 's bidding , and , stand one day by the window , she look away into the far distance a if she be very sad .
` Why be you stand there look so sad ? '
ask the Hunter .
` Alas , my love , ' she reply , ` over there lie the granite mountain where the costly precious stone grow .
I have a great longing to go there , so that when I think of it I be very sad .
For who can fetch them ?
Only the bird who fly ; a man , never . '
` If you have no other trouble , ' say the Hunter , ` that one I can easily remove from your heart . '
So he wrap her round in his cloak and wish themselves to the granite mountain , and in an instant there they be , sit on it !
The precious stone sparkle so brightly on all side that it be a pleasure to see them , and they collect the most beautiful and costly together .
But now the old witch have through her cause the Hunter 's eye to become heavy .
He say to the maiden , ` We will sit down for a little while and rest ; I be so tired that I can hardly stand on my foot . '
So they sit down , and he lay his head on her lap and fell asleep .
As soon a he be sound asleep she unfasten the cloak from his shoulder , throw it on her own , leave the granite and stone , and wish herself home again .
But when the Hunter have finish his sleep and awoke , he find that his love have betray him and leave him alone on the wild mountain .
` Oh , ' say he , ` why be faithlessness so great in the world ? '
and he sit down in sorrow and trouble , not know what to do .
But the mountain belong to fierce and huge giant , who live on it and trade there , and he have not sit long before he saw three of them stride towards him .
So he lay down as if he have fall into a deep sleep .
The giant come up , and the first push him with his foot , and say , ` What sort of an earthworm be that ? '
The second say , ` Crush him dead . '
But the third say contemptuously , ` It be not worth the trouble !
Let him live ; he can not remain here , and if he go high up the mountain the cloud will take him and carry him off . '
Talking thus they go away .
But the Hunter have listen to their talk , and as soon a they have go he rise and climb to the summit .
When he have sit there a little while a cloud sweep by , and , seize him , carry him away .
It travel for a time in the sky , and then it sink down and hover over a large vegetable garden surround by wall , so that he come safely to the ground amidst cabbage and vegetable .
The Hunter then look about him , say , ` If only I have something to eat !
I be so hungry , and it will go badly with me in the future , for I see here not an apple or pear or fruit of any kind -- nothing but vegetable everywhere . '
At last he think , ` At a pinch I can eat a salad ; it do not taste particularly nice , but it will refresh me . '
So he look about for a good head and ate it , but no sooner have he swallow a couple of mouthful than he felt very strange , and find himself wonderfully change .
Four leg begin to grow on him , a thick head , and two long ear , and he saw with horror that he have change into a donkey .
But a he be still very hungry and this juicy salad taste very good to his present nature , he go on eat with a still great appetite .
At last he get hold of another kind of cabbage , but scarcely have swallow it when he felt another change , and he once more regain his human form .
The Hunter now lay down and sleep off his weariness .
When he awake the next morning he break off a head of the bad and a head of the good cabbage , thinking , ` This will help me to regain my own , and to punish faithlessness . '
Then he put the head in his pocket , climb the wall , and start off to seek the castle of his love .
When he have wander about for a couple of day he find it quite easily .
He then brown his face quickly , so that his own mother would not have know him , and go into the castle , where he beg for a lodging . '
I be so tired , ' he say , ' I can go no farther . '
The witch ask , ` Countryman , who be you , and what be your business ? '
He answer , ' I be a messenger of the King , and have be send to seek the fine salad that grow under the sun .
I have be so lucky a to find it , and be bring it with me ; but the heat of the sun be so great that the tender cabbage threaten to grow soft , and I do not know if I shall be able to bring it any far . '
When the old witch heard of the fine salad she want to eat it , and say , ` Dear countryman , just let me taste the wonderful salad . '
` Why not ? '
he answer ; ' I have bring two head with me , and will give you one . '
So say , he open his sack and give her the bad one .
The witch suspect no evil , and her mouth water to taste the new dish , so that she go into the kitchen to prepare it herself .
When it be ready she could not wait till it be serve at the table , but she immediately take a couple of leaf and put them in her mouth .
No sooner , however , have she swallow them than she lose human form , and run into the courtyard in the shape of a donkey .
Now the servant come into the kitchen , and when she saw the salad standing there ready cook she be about to carry it up , but on the way , accord to her old habit , she taste it and eat a couple of leaf .
Immediately the charm work , and she become a donkey , and run out to join the old witch , and the dish with the salad in it fell to the ground .
In the meantime , the messenger be sit with the lovely maiden , and a no one come with the salad , and she want very much to taste it , she say , ' I do n't know where the salad be . '
Then think the Hunter , ` The cabbage must have already begin to work . '
And he say , ' I will go to the kitchen and fetch it myself . '
When he come there he saw the two donkey run about in the courtyard , but the salad be lie on the ground .
` That 's all right , ' say he ; ` two have have their share ! '
And lift the remain leave up , he lay them on the dish and bring them to the maiden . '
I be bring you the delicious food my own self , ' he say , ` so that you need not wait any long . '
Then she eat , and , a the others have do , she at once lose her human form , and run a a donkey into the yard .
When the Hunter have wash his face , so that the change one might know him , he go into the yard , say , ` Now you shall receive a reward for your faithlessness . '
He tie them all three with a rope , and drive them away till he come to a mill .
He knock at the window , and the miller put his head out and ask what he want . '
I have three tiresome animal , ' he answer , ` which I do n't want to keep any long .
If you will take them , give them food and stabling , and do a I tell you with them , I will pay you as much a you want . '
The miller reply , ` Why not ?
What shall I do with them ? '
Then the Hunter say that to the old donkey , which be the witch , three beating and one meal ; to the young one , which be the servant , one beating and three meal ; and to the young one , which be the maiden , no beating and three meal ; for he could not find it in his heart to let the maiden be beat .
Then he go back into the castle , and he find there all that he want .
After a couple of day the miller come and say that he must tell him that the old donkey which be to have three beating and only one meal have die .
` The two others , ' he add , ` be certainly not dead , and get their three meal every day , but they be so sad that they can not last much longer . '
Then the Hunter take pity on them , lay aside his anger , and tell the miller to drive them back again .
And when they come he give them some of the good cabbage to eat , so that they become human again .
Then the beautiful maiden fell on her knee before him , say , ` Oh , my dear , forgive me the ill I have do you !
My mother compel me to do it ; it be against my will , for I love you dearly .
Your wishing-cloak be hang in a cupboard , and a for the bird-heart I will make a drink and give it back to you . '
But he change his mind , and say , ` Keep it ; it make no difference , for I will take you to be my own dear true wife . '
And the wedding be celebrate , and they live happy together till death .
THE LITTLE GREEN FROG -LRB- 8 -RRB- -LRB- 8 -RRB- Cabinet de Fees .
In a part of the world whose name I forget lived once upon a time two king , call Peridor and Diamantino .
They be cousin as well a neighbour , and both be under the protection of the fairy ; though it be only fair to say that the fairy do not love them half so well a their wife do .
Now it often happen that a prince can generally manage to get their own way it be hard for them to be good than it be for common people .
So it be with Peridor and Diamantino ; but of the two , the fairy declare that Diamantino be much the bad ; indeed , he behave so badly to his wife Aglantino , that the fairy would not allow him to live any long ; and he die , leave behind him a little daughter .
As she be an only child , of course this little girl be the heiress of the kingdom , but , be still only a baby , her mother , the widow of Diamantino , be proclaim regent .
The Queen-dowager be wise and good , and try her best to make her people happy .
The only thing she have to vex her be the absence of her daughter ; for the fairy , for reason of their own , determine to bring up the little Princess Serpentine among themselves .
As to the other King , he be really fond of his wife , Queen Constance , but he often grieve her by his thoughtless way , and in order to punish him for his carelessness , the fairy cause her to die quite suddenly .
When she be go the King felt how much he have love her , and his grief be so great -LRB- though he never neglect his duty -RRB- that his subject call him Peridor the Sorrowful .
It seem hardly possible that any man should live like Peridor for fifteen year plunge in such depth of grief , and most likely he would have die too if it have not be for the fairy .
The one comfort the poor King have be his son , Prince Saphir , who be only three year old at the time of his mother 's death , and great care be give to his education .
By the time he be fifteen Saphir have learn everything that a prince should know , and he be , besides , charm and agreeable .
It be about this time that the fairy suddenly take fright l his love for his father should interfere with the plan they have make for the young prince .
So , to prevent this , they place in a pretty little room of which Saphir be very fond a little mirror in a black frame , such a be often bring from Venice .
The Prince do not notice for some day that there be anything new in the room , but at last he perceive it , and go up to look at it more closely .
What be his surprise to see reflect in the mirror , not his own face , but that of a young girl as lovely a the morning !
And , good still , every movement of the girl , just grow out of childhood , be also reflect in the wonderful glass .
As might have be expect , the young Prince lose his heart completely to the beautiful image , and it be impossible to get him out of the room , so busy be he in watch the lovely unknown .
Certainly it be very delightful to be able to see her whom he love at any moment he choose , but his spirit sometimes sink when he wonder what be to be the end of this adventure .
The magic mirror have be for about a year in the Prince 's possession , when one day a new subject of disquiet seize upon him .
As usual , he be engage in look at the girl , when suddenly he think he saw a second mirror reflect in the first , exactly like his own , and with the same power .
And in this he be perfectly right .
The young girl have only possess it for a short time , and neglect all her duty for the sake of the mirror .
Now it be not difficult for Saphir to guess the reason of the change in her , nor why the new mirror be consult so often ; but try a he would he could never see the face of the person who be reflect in it , for the young girl 's figure always come between .
All he know be that the face be that of a man , and this be quite enough to make him madly jealous .
This be the do of the fairy , and we must suppose that they have their reason for act a they do .
When these thing happen Saphir be about eighteen year old , and fifteen year have pass away since the death of his mother .
King Peridor have grow more and more unhappy a time go on , and at last he fell so ill that it seem a if his day be number .
He be so much beloved by his subject that this sad news be hear with despair by the nation , and more than all by the Prince .
During his whole illness the King never speak of anything but the Queen , his sorrow at have grieve her , and his hope of one day see her again .
All the doctor and all the water-cures in the kingdom have be try , and nothing would do him any good .
At last he persuade them to let him lie quietly in his room , where no one come to trouble him .
Perhaps the bad pain he have to bear be a sort of weight on his chest , which make it very hard for him to breathe .
So he command his servant to leave the window open in order that he might get more air .
One day , when he have be leave alone for a few minute , a bird with brilliant plumage come and flutter round the window , and finally rest on the sill .
His feather be sky-blue and gold , his foot and his beak of such glitter ruby that no one could bear to look at them , his eye make the bright diamond look dull , and on his head he wear a crown .
I can not tell you what the crown be make of , but I be quite certain that it be still more splendid than all the rest .
As to his voice I can say nothing about that , for the bird never sing at all .

THE SEVEN-HEADED SERPENT -LRB- 9 -RRB- -LRB- 9 -RRB- ` Die Siebenkopfige Schlange , ' from Schmidt 's Griechische Mahrchen .
Once upon a time there be a king who determine to take a long voyage .
He assemble his fleet and all the seaman , and set out .
They go straight on night and day , until they come to an island which be cover with large tree , and under every tree lay a lion .
As soon a the King have land his men , the lion all rise up together and try to devour them .
After a long battle they manage to overcome the wild beast , but the great number of the men be kill .
Those who remain alive now go on through the forest and find on the other side of it a beautiful garden , in which all the plant of the world flourish together .
There be also in the garden three spring : the first flow with silver , the second with gold , and the third with pearl .
The men unbuckle their knapsack and fill them with those precious thing .
In the middle of the garden they find a large lake , and when they reach the edge of it the Lake begin to speak , and say to them , ` What men be you , and what bring you here ?
Are you come to visit our king ? '
But they be too much frighten to answer .
Then the Lake say , ` You do well to be afraid , for it be at your peril that you be come hither .
Our king , who have seven head , be now asleep , but in a few minute he will wake up and come to me to take his bath !
Woe to anyone who meet him in the garden , for it be impossible to escape from him .
This be what you must do if you wish to save your life .
Take off your clothes and spread them on the path which lead from here to the castle .
The King will then glide over something soft , which he like very much , and he will be so pleased with that that he will not devour you .
He will give you some punishment , but then he will let you go . '
The men do a the Lake advise them , and wait for a time .
At noon the earth begin to quake , and open in many place , and out of the opening appear lion , tiger , and other wild beast , which surround the castle , and thousand and thousand of beast come out of the castle follow their king , the Seven-headed Serpent .
The Serpent glide over the clothes which be spread for him , come to the Lake , and ask it who have strew those soft thing on the path ?
The Lake answer that it have be do by people who have come to do him homage .
The King command that the men should be bring before him .
They come humbly on their knee , and in a few word tell him their story .
Then he speak to them with a mighty and terrible voice , and say , ` Because you have dare to come here , I lay upon you the punishment .
Every year you must bring me from among your people twelve youth and twelve maiden , that I may devour them .
If you do not do this , I will destroy your whole nation . '
Then he desire one of his beast to show the men the way out of the garden , and dismiss them .
They then leave the island and go back to their own country , where they relate what have happen to them .
Soon the time come round when the king of the beast would expect the youth and maiden to be bring to him .
The King therefore issue a proclamation invite twelve youth and twelve maiden to offer themselves up to save their country ; and immediately many young people , far more than enough , hasten to do so .
A new ship be build , and set with black sail , and in it the youth and maiden who be appoint for the king of the beast embark and set out for his country .
When they arrive there they go at once to the Lake , and this time the lion do not stir , nor do the spring flow , and neither do the Lake speak .
So they wait then , and it be not long before the earth quake even more terribly than the first time .
The Seven-headed Serpent come without his train of beast , saw his prey wait for him , and devour it at one mouthful .
Then the ship 's crew return home , and the same thing happen yearly until many year have pass .
Now the King of this unhappy country be grow old , and so be the Queen , and they have no child .
One day the Queen be sit at the window weep bitterly because she be childless , and know that the crown would therefore pas to stranger after the King 's death .
Suddenly a little old woman appear before her , hold an apple in her hand , and say , ` Why do you weep , my Queen , and what make you so unhappy ? '
` Alas , good mother , ' answer the Queen , ' I be unhappy because I have no child . '
` Is that what vexes you ? '
say the old woman .
` Listen to me .
I be a nun from the Spinning Convent , -LRB- 10 -RRB- and my mother when she die leave me this apple .
Whoever eat this apple shall have a child . '
-LRB- 10 -RRB- Convent Gnothi .
The Queen give money to the old woman , and buy the apple from her .
Then she peel it , eat it , and throw the rind out of the window , and it so happen that a mare that be run loose in the court below ate up the rind .
After a time the Queen have a little boy , and the mare also have a male foal .
The boy and the foal grow up together and love each other like brother .
In course of time the King die , and so do the Queen , and their son , who be now nineteen year old , be leave alone .
One day , when he and his horse be talk together , the Horse say to him , ` Listen to me , for I love you and wish for your good and that of the country .
If you go on every year send twelve youth and twelve maiden to the King of the Beasts , your country will very soon be ruin .
Mount upon my back : I will take you to a woman who can direct you how to kill the Seven-headed Serpent . '
Then the youth mount his horse , who carry him far away to a mountain which be hollow , for in it side be a great underground cavern .
In the cavern sit an old woman spinning .
This be the cloister of the nun , and the old woman be the Abbess .
They all spend their time in spinning , and that be why the convent have this name .
All round the wall of the cavern there be bed cut out of the solid rock , upon which the nun slept , and in the middle a light be burn .
It be the duty of the nun to watch the light in turn , that it might never go out , and if anyone of them let it go out the others put her to death .
As soon a the King 's son saw the old Abbess spinning he throw himself at her foot and entreat her to tell him how he could kill the Seven-headed Serpent .
She make the youth rise , embrace him , and say , ` Know , my son , that it be I who send the nun to your mother and cause you to be bear , and with you the horse , with whose help you will be able to free the world from the monster .

With this sword only it be possible to kill the Serpent , because even if it blade break a new one will grow again for every head the monster have .
Thus you will be able to cut off all his seven head .
And this you must also do in order to deceive the King : you must slip into his bed-chamber very softly , and stop up all the bell which be round his bed with cotton .
Then take down the sword gently , and quickly give the monster a blow on his tail with it .
This will make him waken up , and if he catch sight of you he will seize you .
But you must quickly cut off his first head , and then wait till the next one come up .
Then strike it off also , and so go on till you have cut off all his seven head . '
The old Abbess then give the Prince her blessing , and he set out upon his enterprise , arrive at the Serpent 's castle by follow the secret passage which she have show him , and by carefully attend to all her direction he happily succeed in kill the monster .

Thus he free his country from this terrible oppression .
THE GRATEFUL BEASTS -LRB- 11 -RRB- -LRB- 11 -RRB- From the Hungarian .
Kletke .
There be once upon a time a man and woman who have three fine-looking son , but they be so poor that they have hardly enough food for themselves , let alone their child .
So the son determine to set out into the world and to try their luck .
Before start their mother give them each a loaf of bread and her blessing , and have take a tender farewell of her and their father the three set forth on their travel .
The young of the three brother , whose name be Ferko , be a beautiful youth , with a splendid figure , blue eye , fair hair , and a complexion like milk and rose .
His two brother be a jealous of him a they could be , for they think that with his good look he would be sure to be more fortunate than they would ever be .

Their word rejoice Ferko 's heart , and he wait impatiently till even should come and he could rub the precious dew on his sightless eye .

Ferko recognise the queen bee , and say , ` Alas !
how could you help me ?
for I have be set to do a task which no one in the whole world could do , let him be ever such a genius !
To-morrow I must build a palace more beautiful than the King 's , and it must be finish before even . '
` Is that all ? '
answer the bee , ` then you may comfort yourself ; for before the sun go down to-morrow night a palace shall be build unlike any that King have dwell in before .
Just stay here till I come again and tell you that it be finish . '
Having say this she fly merrily away , and Ferko , reassure by her word , lay down on the grass and sleep peacefully till the next morning .
Early on the following day the whole town be on it foot , and everyone wonder how and where the stranger would build the wonderful palace .
The Princess alone be silent and sorrowful , and have cry all night till her pillow be wet , so much do she take the fate of the beautiful youth to heart .
Ferko spend the whole day in the meadow wait the return of the bee .
And when evening be come the queen bee flew by , and perch on his shoulder she say , ` The wonderful palace be ready .
Be of good cheer , and lead the King to the hill just outside the city wall . '
And hum gaily she fly away again .
Ferko go at once to the King and tell him the palace be finish .
The whole court go out to see the wonder , and their astonishment be great at the sight which meet their eye .
A splendid palace rear itself on the hill just outside the wall of the city , make of the most exquisite flower that ever grow in mortal garden .
The roof be all of crimson rose , the window of lily , the wall of white carnation , the floor of glow auricula and violet , the door of gorgeous tulip and narcissus with sunflower for knocker , and all round hyacinth and other sweet-smelling flower bloom in mass , so that the air be perfume far and near and enchant all who be present .
This splendid palace have be build by the grateful queen bee , who have summon all the other bee in the kingdom to help her .
The King 's amazement know no bound , and the Princess 's eye beam with delight a she turn them from the wonderful building on the delighted Ferko .
But the two brother have grow quite green with envy , and only declare the more that Ferko be nothing but a wicked magician .
The King , although he have be surprise and astonish at the way his command have be carry out , be very vexed that the stranger should escape with his life , and turn to the two brother he say , ` He have certainly accomplish the first task , with the aid no doubt of his diabolical magic ; but what shall we give him to do now ?
Let u make it as difficult a possible , and if he fail he shall die . '
Then the eldest brother reply , ` The corn have all be cut , but it have not yet be put into barn ; let the knave collect all the grain in the kingdom into one big heap before to-morrow night , and if as much a a stalk of corn be leave let him be put to death .
The Princess grow white with terror when she hear these word ; but Ferko felt much more cheerful than he have do the first time , and wander out into the meadow again , wonder how he be to get out of the difficulty .
But he could think of no way of escape .
The sun sink to rest and night come on , when a little mouse start out of the grass at Ferko 's foot , and say to him , ` I 'm delighted to see you , my kind benefactor ; but why be you look so sad ?
Can I be of any help to you , and thus repay your great kindness to me ? '
Then Ferko recognise the mouse whose front paw he have heal , and reply , ` Alas I how can you help me in a matter that be beyond any human power !
Before to-morrow night all the grain in the kingdom have to be gather into one big heap , and if as much a a stalk of corn be want I must pay for it with my life . '
` Is that all ? '
answer the mouse ; ` that need n't distress you much .
Just trust in me , and before the sun set again you shall hear that your task be do . '
And with these word the little creature scamper away into the field .
Ferko , who never doubt that the mouse would be as good a it word , lay down comfort on the soft grass and sleep soundly till next morning .
The day pass slowly , and with the evening come the little mouse and say , ` Now there be not a single stalk of corn leave in any field ; they be all collect in one big heap on the hill out there . '
Then Ferko go joyfully to the King and tell him that all he demand have be do .
And the whole Court go out to see the wonder , and be no less astonish than they have be the first time .
For in a heap high than the King 's palace lay all the grain of the country , and not a single stalk of corn have be leave behind in any of the field .
And how have all this be do ?
The little mouse have summon every other mouse in the land to it help , and together they have collect all the grain in the kingdom .
The King could not hide his amazement , but at the same time his wrath increase , and he be more ready than ever to believe the two brother , who keep on repeat that Ferko be nothing more nor less than a wicked magician .
Only the beautiful Princess rejoice over Ferko 's success , and look on him with friendly glance , which the youth return .
The more the cruel King gaze on the wonder before him , the more angry he become , for he could not , in the face of his promise , put the stranger to death .
He turn once more to the two brother and say , ` His diabolical magic have help him again , but now what third task shall we set him to do ?
No matter how impossible it be , he must do it or die . '
The eldest answered quickly , ` Let him drive all the wolf of the kingdom on to this hill before to-morrow night .
If he do this he may go free ; if not he shall be hang a you have say . '
At these word the Princess burst into tear , and when the King saw this he order her to be shut up in a high tower and carefully guard till the dangerous magician should either have leave the kingdom or be hang on the near tree .
Ferko wander out into the field again , and sit down on the stump of a tree wonder what he should do next .
Suddenly a big wolf run up to him , and stand still say , ` I 'm very glad to see you again , my kind benefactor .
What be you think about all alone by yourself ?
If I can help you in any way only say the word , for I would like to give you a proof of my gratitude . '
Ferko at once recognise the wolf whose broken leg he have heal , and tell him what he have to do the following day if he wish to escape with his life .
` But how in the world , ' he add , ` be I to collect all the wolf of the kingdom on to that hill over there ? '
` If that 's all you want do , ' answer the wolf , ` you need n't worry yourself .
I 'll undertake the task , and you 'll hear from me again before sunset to-morrow .
Keep your spirit up . '
And with these word he trot quickly away .
Then the youth rejoice greatly , for now he felt that his life be safe ; but he grow very sad when he think of the beautiful Princess , and that he would never see her again if he leave the country .
He lay down once more on the grass and soon fell fast asleep .
All the next day he spend wander about the field , and toward even the wolf come run to him in a great hurry and say , ' I have collect together all the wolf in the kingdom , and they be wait for you in the wood .
Go quickly to the King , and tell him to go to the hill that he may see the wonder you have do with his own eye .
Then return at once to me and get on my back , and I will help you to drive all the wolf together . '
Then Ferko go straight to the palace and tell the King that he be ready to perform the third task if he would come to the hill and see it do .
Ferko himself return to the field , and mount on the wolf 's back he ride to the wood close by .
Quick a lightning the wolf fly round the wood , and in a minute many hundred wolf rise up before him , increase in number every moment , till they could be count by thousand .
He drive them all before him on to the hill , where the King and his whole Court and Ferko 's two brother be stand .
Only the lovely Princess be not present , for she be shut up in her tower weep bitterly .
The wicked brother stamp and foam with rage when they saw the failure of their wicked design .
But the King be overcome by a sudden terror when he saw the enormous pack of wolf approach nearer and nearer , and call out to Ferko he say , ` Enough , enough , we do n't want any more . '
But the wolf on whose back Ferko sat , say to it rider , ` Go on !
go on ! '
and at the same moment many more wolf run up the hill , howl horribly and show their white teeth .
The King in his terror call out , ` Stop a moment ; I will give you half my kingdom if you will drive all the wolf away . '
But Ferko pretend not to hear , and drive some more thousand before him , so that everyone quake with horror and fear .
Then the King raise his voice again and call out , ` Stop !
you shall have my whole kingdom , if you will only drive these wolf back to the place they come from . '
But the wolf keep on encourage Ferko , and say , ` Go on !
go on ! '
So he lead the wolf on , till at last they fell on the King and on the wicked brother , and eat them and the whole Court up in a moment .
Then Ferko go straight to the palace and set the Princess free , and on the same day he marry her and be crown King of the country .
And the wolf all go peacefully back to their own home , and Ferko and his bride live for many year in peace and happiness together , and be much beloved by great and small in the land .
THE GIANTS AND THE HERD-BOY -LRB- 12 -RRB- -LRB- 12 -RRB- From the Bukowniaer .
Von Wliolocki .
There be once upon a time a poor boy who have neither father nor mother .
In order to gain a living he look after the sheep of a great Lord .
Day and night he spend out in the open field , and only when it be very wet and stormy do he take refuge in a little hut on the edge of a big forest .
Now one night , when he be sit on the grass beside his flock , he hear not very far from him the sound a of some one cry .
He rise up and follow the direction of the noise .
To his dismay and astonishment he find a Giant lying at the entrance of the wood ; he be about to run off as fast a his leg could carry him , when the Giant call out : ` Do n't be afraid , I wo n't harm you .
On the contrary , I will reward you handsomely if you will bind up my foot .
I hurt it when I be try to root up an oak-tree . '
The Herd-boy take off his shirt , and bind up the Giant 's wounded foot with it .
Then the Giant rise up and say , ` Now come and I will reward you .
We be go to celebrate a marriage to-day , and I promise you we shall have plenty of fun .
Come and enjoy yourself , but in order that my brother may n't see you , put this band round your waist and then you 'll be invisible . '
With these word he hand the Herd-boy a belt , and walk on in front he lead him to a fountain where hundred of Giants and Giantesses be assemble prepare to hold a wedding .
They dance and play different game till midnight ; then one of the Giants tear up a plant by it root , and all the Giants and Giantesses make themselves so thin that they disappear into the earth through the hole make by the uprooting of the plant .
The wounded Giant remain behind to the last and call out , ` Herd-boy , where be you ? '
` Here I be , close to you , ' be the reply .
` Touch me , ' say the Giant , ` so that you too may come with u under ground . '
The Herd-boy do a he be tell , and before he could have believe it possible he find himself in a big hall , where even the wall be make of pure gold .
Then to his astonishment he saw that the hall be furnish with the table and chair that belong to his master .
In a few minute the company begin to eat and drink .
The banquet be a very gorgeous one , and the poor youth fell to and eat and drink lustily .
When he have eat and drink as much a he could he think to himself , ` Why should n't I put a loaf of bread in my pocket ?
I shall be glad of it to-morrow . '
So he seize a loaf when no one be look and stow it away under his tunic .
No sooner have he do so than the wounded Giant limp up to him and whisper softly , ` Herd-boy , where be you ? '
` Here I be , ' reply the youth .
` Then hold on to me , ' say the Giant , ` so that I may lead you up above again . '
So the Herd-boy hold on to the Giant , and in a few moment he find himself on the earth once more , but the Giant have vanish .
The Herd-boy return to his sheep , and take off the invisible belt which he hide carefully in his bag .
The next morning the lad felt hungry , and think he would cut off a piece of the loaf he have carry away from the Giants ' wedding feast , and eat it .
But although he try with all his might , he could n't cut off the small piece .
Then in despair he bite the loaf , and what be his astonishment when a piece of gold fell out of his mouth and roll at his foot .
He bite the bread a second and third time , and each time a piece of gold fell out of his mouth ; but the bread remain untouched .
The Herd-boy be very much delight over his stroke of good fortune , and , hide the magic loaf in his bag , he hurry off to the near village to buy himself something to eat , and then return to his sheep .
Now the Lord whose sheep the Herd-boy look after have a very lovely daughter , who always smile and nod to the youth when she walk with her father in his field .
For a long time the Herd-boy have make up his mind to prepare a surprise for this beautiful creature on her birthday .
So when the day approach he put on his invisible belt , take a sack of gold piece with him , and slip into her room in the middle of the night , he place the bag of gold beside her bed and return to his sheep .
The girl 's joy be great , and so be her parent ' next day when they find the sack full of gold piece .
The Herd-boy be so pleased to think what pleasure he have give that the next night he place another bag of gold beside the girl 's bed .
And this he continue to do for seven night , and the girl and her parent make up their mind that it must be a good Fairy who bring the gold every night .
But one night they determine to watch , and see from their hiding place who the bringer of the sack of gold really be .
On the eighth night a fearful storm of wind and rain come on while the Herd-boy be on his way to bring the beautiful girl another bag of gold .
Then for the first time he notice , just a he reach his master 's house , that he have forget the belt which make him invisible .
He do n't like the idea of go back to his hut in the wind and wet , so he just step a he be into the girl 's room , lay the sack of gold beside her , and be turn to leave the room , when his master confront him and say , ` You young rogue , so you be go to steal the gold that a good Fairy bring every night , be you ? '
The Herd-boy be so take aback by his word , that he stand tremble before him , and do not dare to explain his presence .
Then his master speak .
` As you have hitherto always behave well in my service I will not send you to prison ; but leave your place instantly and never let me see your face again . '
So the Herd-boy go back to his hut , and take his loaf and belt with him , he go to the near town .
There he buy himself some fine clothes , and a beautiful coach with four horse , hire two servant , and drive back to his master .
You may imagine how astonished he be to see his Herd-boy returning to him in this manner !
Then the youth tell him of the piece of good luck that have befall him , and ask him for the hand of his beautiful daughter .
This be readily grant , and the two live in peace and happiness to the end of their life .
THE INVISIBLE PRINCE Once upon a time there live a Fairy who have power over the earth , the sea , fire , and the air ; and this Fairy have four son .
The eldest , who be quick and lively , with a vivid imagination , she make Lord of Fire , which be in her opinion the noble of all the element .
To the second son , whose wisdom and prudence make amends for his be rather dull , she give the government of the earth .
The third be wild and savage , and of monstrous stature ; and the Fairy , his mother , who be ashamed of his defect , hop to hide them by create him King of the Seas .
The young , who be the slave of his passion and of a very uncertain temper , become Prince of the Air .
Being the young , he be naturally his mother 's favourite ; but this do not blind her to his weakness , and she foresee that some day he would suffer much pain through fall in love .
So she think the best thing she could do be to bring him up with a horror of woman ; and , to her great delight , she saw this dislike only increase a he grow old .
From his early childhood he hear nothing but story of prince who have fall into all sort of trouble through love ; and she draw such terrible picture of poor little Cupid that the young man have no difficulty in believe that he be the root of all evil .
All the time that this wise mother could spare from fill her son with hatred for all womenkind she pass in give him a love of the pleasure of the chase , which henceforth become his chief joy .
For his amusement she have make a new forest , plant with the most splendid tree , and turn loose in it every animal that could be find in any of the four quarter of the globe .
In the midst of this forest she build a palace which have not it equal for beauty in the whole world , and then she consider that she have do enough to make any prince happy .
Now it be all very well to abuse the God of Love , but a man can not struggle against his fate .
In his secret heart the Prince get tire of his mother 's constant talk on this subject ; and when one day she quit the palace to attend to some business , beg him never to go beyond the ground , he at once jump at the chance of disobey her .
Left to himself the Prince soon forget the wise counsel of his mother , and feel very much bore with his own company , he order some of the spirit of the air to carry him to the court of a neighbouring sovereign .
This kingdom be situate in the Island of Roses , where the climate be so delicious that the grass be always green and the flower always sweet .
The wave , instead of beat on the rock , seem to die gently on the shore ; cluster of golden bush cover the land , and the vine be bent low with grape .
The King of this island have a daughter name Rosalie , who be more lovely than any girl in the whole world .
No sooner have the eye of the Prince of the Air rest on her than he forget all the terrible woe which have be prophesy to him ever since he be bear , for in one single moment the plan of year be often upset .
He instantly begin to think how best to make himself happy , and the short way that occur to him be to have Rosalie carry off by his attendant spirit .
It be easy to imagine the feeling of the King when he find that his daughter have vanish .
He weep her loss night and day , and his only comfort be to talk over it with a young and unknown prince , who have just arrive at the Court .
Alas !
he do not know what a deep interest the stranger have in Rosalie , for he too have see her , and have fall a victim to her charm .
One day the King , more sorrowful than usual , be walk sadly along the sea-shore , when after a long silence the unknown Prince , who be his only companion , suddenly speak .
` There be no evil without a remedy , ' he say to the unhappy father ; ` and if you will promise me your daughter in marriage , I will undertake to bring her back to you . '
` You be try to soothe me by vain promise , ' answer the King .
` Did I not see her caught up into the air , in spite of cry which would have soften the heart of any one but the barbarian who have rob me of her ?
The unfortunate girl be pin away in some unknown land , where perhaps no foot of man have ever tread , and I shall see her no more .
But go , generous stranger ; bring back Rosalie if you can , and live happy with her ever after in this country , of which I now declare you heir . '
Although the stranger 's name and rank be unknown to Rosalie 's father , he be really the son of the King of the Golden Isle , which have for capital a city that extend from one sea to another .
The wall , wash by the quiet water , be cover with gold , which make one think of the yellow sand .
Above them be a rampart of orange and lemon tree , and all the street be pave with gold .
The King of this beautiful island have one son , for whom a life of adventure have be foretell at his birth .
This so frightened his father and mother that in order to comfort them a Fairy , who happen to be present at the time , produce a little pebble which she tell them to keep for the Prince till he grow up , a by put it in his mouth he would become invisible , as long a he do not try to speak , for if he do the stone would lose all it virtue .
In this way the good fairy hop that the Prince would be protect against all danger .
No sooner do the Prince begin to grow out of boyhood than he long to see if the other country of the world be as splendid a the one in which he live .
So , under pretence of visit some small island that belong to his father , he set out .
But a frightful storm drive his ship on to unknown shore , where most of his follower be put to death by the savage , and the Prince himself only manage to escape by make use of his magic pebble .
By this mean he pass through the midst of them unseen , and wander on till he reach the coast , where he re-embarked on board his ship .
The first land he sight be the Island of Roses , and he go at once to the court of the King , Rosalie 's father .
The moment his eye behold the Princess , he fell in love with her like everyone else .
He have already spend several month in this condition when the Prince of the Air whirl her away , to the grief and despair of every man on the island .
But sad though everybody be , the Prince of the Golden Isle be perfectly inconsolable , and he pass both day and night in bemoan his loss .
` Alas ! '
he cry ; ` shall I never see my lovely Princess again ? '
Who know where she may be , and what fairy may have her in his keep ?
I be only a man , but I be strong in my love , and I will seek the whole world through till I find her . '
So say , he leave the court , and make ready for his journey .
He travel many weary day without hear a single word of the lost Princess , till one morning , a he be walk through a thick forest , he suddenly perceive a magnificent palace stand at the end of a pine avenue , and his heart bound to think that he might be gaze on Rosalie 's prison .
He hasten his step , and quickly arrive at the gate of the palace , which be form of a single agate .
The gate swung open to let him through , and he next pass successively three court , surround by deep ditch fill with running water , with bird of brilliant plumage fly about the bank .
Everything around be rare and beautiful , but the Prince scarcely raise his eye to all these wonder .
He think only of the Princess and where he should find her , but in vain he open every door and search in every corner ; he neither saw Rosalie nor anyone else .
At last there be no place leave for him to search but a little wood , which contain in the centre a sort of hall build entirely of orange-trees , with four small room open out of the corner .
Three of these be empty except for statue and wonderful thing , but in the fourth the Invisible Prince catch sight of Rosalie .
His joy at behold her again be , however , somewhat lessen by see that the Prince of the Air be kneel at her foot , and plead his own cause .
But it be in vain that he implore her to listen ; she only shake her head .
` No , ' be all she would say ; ` you snatch me from my father whom I love , and all the splendour in the world can never console me .
Go !
I can never feel anything towards you but hate and contempt . '
With these word she turn away and enter her own apartment .
Unknown to herself the Invisible Prince have follow her , but fear to be discover by the Princess in the presence of others , he make up his mind to wait quietly till dark ; and employ the long hour in write a poem to the Princess , which he lay on the bed beside her .
This do , he think of nothing but how best to deliver Rosalie , and he resolve to take advantage of a visit which the Prince of the Air pay every year to his mother and brother in order to strike the blow .
One day Rosalie be sit alone in her room thinking of her trouble when she suddenly saw a pen get up from off the desk and begin to write all by itself on a sheet of white paper .
As she do not know that it be guide by an invisible hand she be very much astonish , and the moment that the pen have cease to move she instantly go over to the table , where she find some lovely verse , tell her that another share her distress , whatever they might be , and love her with all his heart ; and that he would never rest until he have deliver her from the hand of the man she hat .
Thus encourage , she tell him all her story , and of the arrival of a young stranger in her father 's palace , whose look have so charm her that since that day she have think of no one else .
At these word the Prince could contain himself no longer .
He take the pebble from his mouth , and fling himself at Rosalie 's foot .
When they have get over the first rapture of meet they begin to make plan to escape from the power of the Prince of the Air .
But this do not prove easy , for the magic stone would only serve for one person at a time , and in order to save Rosalie the Prince of the Golden Isle would have to expose himself to the fury of his enemy .
But Rosalie would not hear of this .
` No , Prince , ' she say ; ` since you be here this island no longer feel a prison .
Besides , you be under the protection of a Fairy , who always visit your father 's court at this season .
Go instantly and seek her , and when she be find implore the gift of another stone with similar power .
Once you have that , there will be no further difficulty in the way of escape . '
The Prince of the Air return a few day later from his mother 's palace , but the Invisible Prince have already set out .
He have , however , entirely forget the road by which he have come , and lose himself for so long in the forest , that when at last he reach home the Fairy have already leave , and , in spite of all his grief , there be nothing for it but to wait till the Fairy 's next visit , and allow Rosalie to suffer three month longer .
This think drive him to despair , and he have almost make up his mind to return to the place of her captivity , when one day , a he be stroll along an alley in the wood , he saw a huge oak open it trunk , and out of it step two Princes in earnest conversation .
As our hero have the magic stone in his mouth they imagine themselves alone , and do not lower their voice .
` What ! '
say one , ` be you always go to allow yourself to be torment by a passion which can never end happily , and in your whole kingdom can you find nothing else to satisfy you ? '
` What be the use , ' reply the other , ` of be Prince of the Gnomes , and have a mother who be queen over all the four element , if I can not win the love of the Princess Argentine ?
From the moment that I first saw her , sit in the forest surround by flower , I have never cease to think of her night and day , and , although I love her , I be quite convinced that she will never care for me .
You know that I have in my palace the cabinet of the year .
In the first , great mirror reflect the past ; in the second , we contemplate the present ; in the third , the future can be read .
It be here that I flee after I have gaze on the Princess Argentine , but instead of love I only saw scorn and contempt .
Think how great must be my devotion , when , in spite of my fate , I still love on ! '
Now the Prince of the Golden Isle be enchant with this conversation , for the Princess Argentine be his sister , and he hop , by mean of her influence over the Prince of the Gnomes , to obtain from his brother the release of Rosalie .
So he joyfully return to his father 's palace , where he find his friend the Fairy , who at once present him with a magic pebble like his own .
As may be imagine , he lose no time in set out to deliver Rosalie , and travel so fast that he soon arrive at the forest , in the midst of which she lay a captive .
But though he find the palace he do not find Rosalie .
He hunt high and low , but there be no sign of her , and his despair be so great that he be ready , a thousand time over , to take his own life .
At last he remember the conversation of the two Princes about the cabinet of the year , and that if he could manage to reach the oak tree , he would be certain to discover what have become of Rosalie .
Happily , he soon find out the secret of the passage and enter the cabinet of the present , where he saw reflect in the mirror the unfortunate Rosalie sit on the floor weep bitterly , and surround with genius , who never leave her night or day .
This sight only increase the misery of the Prince , for he do not know where the castle be , nor how to set about find it .
However , he resolve to seek the whole world through till he come to the right place .
He begin by set sail in a favourable wind , but his bad luck follow him even on the sea .
He have scarcely lose sight of the land when a violent storm arose , and after several hour of beat about , the vessel be drive on to some rock , on which it dash itself to bit .
The Prince be fortunate enough to be able to lay hold of a floating spar , and contrive to keep himself afloat ; and , after a long struggle with the wind and wave , he be cast upon a strange island .
But what be his surprise , on reach the shore , to hear sound of the most heartrending distress , mingle with the sweet song which have ever charm him !
His curiosity be instantly rouse , and he advance cautiously till he saw two huge dragon guard the gate of a wood .
They be terrible indeed to look upon .
Their body be cover with glittering scale ; their curly tail extend far over the land ; flame dart from their mouth and nose , and their eye would have make the brave shudder ; but a the Prince be invisible and they do not see him , he slip past them into the wood .
He find himself at once in a labyrinth , and wander about for a long time without meet anyone ; in fact , the only sight he saw be a circle of human hand , stick out of the ground above the wrist , each with a bracelet of gold , on which a name be write .
The farther he advance in the labyrinth the more curious he become , till he be stop by two corps lie in the midst of a cypress alley , each with a scarlet cord round his neck and a bracelet on his arm on which be engrave their own name , and those of two Princesses .
The invisible Prince recognise these dead men a Kings of two large island near his own home , but the name of the Princesses be unknown to him .
He grieve for their unhappy fate , and at once proceed to bury them ; but no sooner have he lay them in their graf , than their hand start up through the earth and remain stick up like those of their fellow .
The Prince go on his way , think about this strange adventure , when suddenly at the turn of the walk he perceive a tall man whose face be the picture of misery , hold in his hand a silken cord of the exact colour of those round the neck of the dead men .
A few step far this man come up with another a miserable to the full a he himself ; they silently embrace , and then without a word pass the cord round their throat , and fell dead side by side .
In vain the Prince rush to their assistance and strive to undo the cord .
He could not loosen it ; so he bury them like the others and continue his path .
He felt , however , that great prudence be necessary , or he himself might become the victim of some enchantment ; and he be thankful to slip past the dragon , and enter a beautiful park , with clear stream and sweet flower , and a crowd of men and maiden .
But he could not forget the terrible thing he have see , and hop eagerly for a clue to the mystery .
Noticing two young people talk together , he draw near think that he might get some explanation of what puzzle him .
And so he do .
` You swear , ' say the Prince , ` that you will love me till you die , but I fear your faithless heart , and I feel that I shall soon have to seek the Fairy Despair , ruler of half this island .
She carry off the lover who have be cast away by their mistress , and wish to have do with life .
She place them in a labyrinth where they be condemn to walk for ever , with a bracelet on their arm and a cord round their neck , unless they meet another as miserable a themselves .
Then the cord be pull and they lie where they fall , till they be bury by the first passer by .

This , she add , do not appear impossible , a it often fly about to some distance in the neighbourhood .
Having tell the Prince all this , the Fairy go out in hope of see the parrot , and soon return with the bird in her hand .
She promptly shut it up in a cage , and , touch the Prince with her wand , transform him into an exactly similar parrot ; after which , she instruct him how to reach the Princess .
The Prince reach the palace in safety , but be so dazzled at first by the Princess 's beauty , which far surpass his expectation , that he be quite dumb for a time .

This soon reassure the Prince , and encourage him to play his part well , and he begin to say a thousand agreeable thing which charm the Princess .
Presently the King appear , and the parrot notice with joy how much he be dislike .

When he saw her well-disposed towards him , he exclaim : ` Madam , I have a most important secret to confide to you , and I beg you not to be alarm by what I be about to say .

There be once upon a time a miller who be very well off , and have a much money and a many good a he know what to do with .

He wander about all day full of despair and misery , and when he lay down at night he could get no rest , but lay awake all night sunk in sorrowful thought .
One morning he rise up before dawn and go outside , for he think his heart would be lighter in the open air .
As he wander up and down on the bank of the mill-pond he hear a rustling in the water , and when he look near he saw a white woman rise up from the wave .
He realise at once that this could be none other than the nixy of the mill-pond , and in his terror he do n't know if he should fly away or remain where he be .

The miller think she must mean one of his puppy or kitten , so promise the nixy at once what she ask , and return to his mill full of hope .
On the threshold he be greet by a servant with the news that his wife have just give birth to a boy .

I would gladly give up all the good fortune she promise me , ' he say , ` if I could only save my child . '
But no one could think of any advice to give him , beyond take care that the child never go near the mill-pond .
So the boy throve and grow big , and in the meantime all prosper with the miller , and in a few year he be rich than he have ever be before .
But all the same he do not enjoy his good fortune , for he could not forget his compact with the nixy , and he know that sooner or later she would demand his fulfilment of it .

Once upon a time there be a Glass Mountain at the top of which stand a castle make of pure gold , and in front of the castle there grow an apple-tree on which there be golden apple .

ALPHEGE , OR THE GREEN MONKEY Many year ago there live a King , who be twice marry .
His first wife , a good and beautiful woman , die at the birth of her little son , and the King her husband be so overwhelmed with grief at her loss that his only comfort be in the sight of his heir .
When the time for the young Prince 's christening come the King chose a godmother a neighbouring Princess , so celebrated for her wisdom and goodness that she be commonly call ` the Good Queen . '
She name the baby Alphege , and from that moment take him to her heart .
Time wipe away the great grief , and after two or three year the King marry again .
His second wife be a Princess of undeniable beauty , but by no mean of so amiable a disposition a the first Queen .
In due time a second Prince be bear , and the Queen be devour with rage at the thought that Prince Alphege come between her son and the throne .
She take care however to conceal her jealous feeling from the King .
At length she could control herself no longer , so she send a trusty servant to her old and faithful friend the Fairy of the Mountain , to beg her to devise some mean by which she might get rid of her stepson .
The Fairy reply that , much a she desire to be agreeable to the Queen in every way , it be impossible for her to attempt anything against the young Prince , who be under the protection of some great Power than her own .
The ` Good Queen ' on her side watch carefully over her godson .
She be oblige to do so from a distance , her own country be a remote one , but she be well inform of all that go on and know all about the Queen 's wicked design .
She therefore send the Prince a large and splendid ruby , with injunction to wear it night and day a it would protect him from all attack , but add that the talisman only retain it power as long a the Prince remain within his father 's dominion .
The Wicked Queen know this make every attempt to get the Prince out of the country , but her effort fail , till one day accident do what she be unable to accomplish .
The King have an only sister who be deeply attach to him , and who be marry to the sovereign of a distant country .
She have always keep up a close correspondence with her brother , and the account she hear of Prince Alphege make her long to become acquainted with so charm a nephew .
She entreat the King to allow the Prince to visit her , and after some hesitation which be overrule by his wife , he finally consent .

When he outgrow her care her husband be appoint a his tutor and governor , so that he have never be separate from this excellent couple , who love him as tenderly a they do their only daughter Zayda , and be warmly love by him in return .
When the Prince set forth on his travel it be but natural that this devoted couple should accompany him , and accordingly he start with them and attend by a numerous retinue .

Indeed , have the King her son not be deservedly beloved a revolution would certainly have arise .

He forbid his courtier to frighten it , and the monkey , notice how much attention be be pay him , sprang from bough to bough , and at length gradually approach the King , who offer him some food .
The monkey take it very daintily and finally come to the table .
The King take him on his knee , and , delight with his capture , bring him home with him .
He would trust no one else with it care , and the whole Court soon talk of nothing but the pretty green monkey .
One morning , a Prince Alphege 's governess and her daughter be alone together , the little monkey sprang in through an open window .
He have escape from the palace , and his manner be so gentle and caress that Zayda and her mother soon get over the first fright he have give them .
He have spend some time with them and quite win their heart by his insinuating way , when the King discover where he be and send to fetch him back .
But the monkey make such piteous cry , and seem so unhappy when anyone attempt to catch him , that the two lady beg the King to leave him a little longer with them , to which he consent .

The following night the elder lady dreamt that she saw the Good Queen , who say , ` Do not weep any long but follow my direction .
Go into your garden and lift up the little marble slab at the foot of the great myrtle tree .

Then she hasten to rouse her daughter and together they prepare the bath , for they would not let their woman know what they be about .

He make careful inquiry into the matter , and think it hardly probable that a quiet widow and a young girl would think of attempt anything of the nature of a revolution .

So say , he respectfully kiss the Prince 's hand .

To clear away any possible doubt , he show the ruby which the Good Queen have give him in his childhood .
As they be gaze at it , it suddenly split with a loud noise , and at the same moment the Wicked Queen expire .
King Alphege lose no time in marry his dear and lovely Zayda , and his joy be complete when the Good Queen appear at his wedding .
She assure him that the Fairy of the Mountain have henceforth lose all power over him , and after spend some time with the young couple , and bestow the most costly present on them , she retire to her own country .
King Alphege insist on his brother share his throne , and they all live to a good old age , universally beloved and admire .
FAIRER-THAN-A-FAIRY Once there live a King who have no child for many year after his marriage .
At length heaven grant him a daughter of such remarkable beauty that he could think of no name so appropriate for her a ` Fairer-than-a-Fairy . '
